2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
About This Report
Report Overview
This Report was published pursuant 
to the Global Reporting Initiative 
Sustainability Reporting Standards 
(GRI Standards) 2021 issued by 
the Global Reporting Initiative 
(GRI) for the period from January 
1, 2022 to December 31, 2022. 
This Report provides an accurate 
and detailed introduction to the 
sustainability actions of Formosa 
Plastics Corporation (hereinafter 
referred to as "FPC") in areas 
including corporate governance, 
environmental sustainability, happy 
enterprise, safe workplace, and 
community co-prosperity.
Publication Overview
 First publication date: December 2015
 Previous publication date: June 2022
 Current version publication date: May 2023
 Next publication date: May 2024
Scope and Boundary of Reporting
The information recorded herein mainly focuses on FPC (please 
refer to 1.2.2 Company History for more details) and does not 
include its investment companies in Taiwan and the U.S and 
subsidiaries in China. Any other information with a different scope 
of the disclosure will be otherwise specified. The data quoted and 
reporting boundary used in the 2022 Sustainable Development 
Report are identical to those in 2021.
The source of the financial information is the public accountant-
certified statement, while other statistics are generally quoted 
from information provided by government departments or 
relevant websites and will be presented normally. Any exceptions 
will be specified.

Management of Sustainability Report
Internal Review
 In accordance with the requirements set forth in the Rules Governing the Preparation and Filing of 
Sustainability Reports by TWSE Listed Companies, FPC formulates procedures for the preparation 
and verification of the sustainability report and incorporates them into the internal control system. 
This Report covers information on the economic, environmental, and social aspects.
 The President's Office compiles the information provided by each unit, and the relevant data 
are reviewed and confirmed by the Sustainable Development Promotion Team of FPC to ensure 
compliance with the principles of integrity and transparency before submitting to the Sustainable 
Development Committee. Upon approval by the Chairman, the final report is disclosed publicly 
and submitted to the Board of Directors in May every year.
External Assurance
 This Report has been verified by the third party certifying company, AFNOR Asia Ltd., and the 
verification results comply with the AA1000AS v3 Type 1 Assurance. Please refer to Appendix 
VI for the Independent Assurance Opinion Statement.
 This Reports has been verified to comply with Materiality, Inclusivity, Responsiveness, and 
Impact of the AA1000 AccountAbility Principles Standard (APS).

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
Progress of Sustainable Development
Response to the United Nations' Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs):
In 2022, FPC aligned nine SDGs and identified 20 targets. SDGs 3, 8, 9, 11, 12, and 13 were relevant to the 
core operations while SDGs 4, 6, and 7 were of secondary relevance. 
Economic
SDGs
Targets

Short-term (1 to 3 years)
FPC's Objectives 
Actions and Achievements in 2022
1. Improve the Company's operating 
performance and pursue 
complete production and sales.
For details of FPC's operating results for 2022, 
please refer to 2.1.1 Operating and Financial 
Performance.
2. Continue to promote production, 
marketing, and research 
operation strategies, develop 
new products and applications 
in collaboration with clients, 
learn about improve product 
quality, and enhance the added 
value of products.
For the actual R&D results of cooperation with 
customers in 2022, please refer to 2.3.2 Product 
R&D and Innovation for details.
3. Promote AI technology 
development and applications.
1. Enhance AI technology development and 
applications toward the five major pillars of 
development. Please refer to 2.3.2 (3) Intelligent 
Management.
2. As of 2022, 175 out of the 336 proposed AI 
technology development cases were completed. 
The remaining 161 AI technology development 
cases are currently ongoing with an expected 
annual benefit of NT$1.03 billion.
4. Expand operations at home 
and abroad and carry out 
debottlenecking projects.
For details, please refer to 2.1.2 Major Investment 
Projects of this Report.
5. Increase the sales volume of 
differentiated products by more 
than 12% compared to 2022.
In 2022, the sales volume of differentiated products 
decreased by 13.6% compared to 2021, not meeting 
the original target (an increase of 6%). Continuous 
efforts will be made.
6. Evaluation and establishment 
of other functional committees 
other than the Audit and 
Remuneration Committee. 
To promote sustainable development efforts, FPC’s 
Board of Directors has approved the establishment 
of the Sustainable Development Committee on 
May 10, 2022, which is composed of 4 independent 
directors. In 2022, a total of two meetings were held.
7. Strengthen the independence 
and supervision mechanism of 
the Board of Directors.
Based on the needs of operation management and in 
order to implement corporate governance practices 
and supervision separately, on March 10, 2023, the 
Board of Directors resolved to promote Senior Vice 
President Mr. Wen-Bee Kuo to Acting President and 
relieve Chairman Mr. Jason Lin of the concurrent 
position of President to strengthen the independence 
of the Board of Directors.

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
Environmental
SDGs
Targets
3.9 / 6.3 / 6.4 / 6.5 /
7.3 / 7.a / 8.4 / 8.8 / 
9.4 / 11.5 / 11.6 /12.2 / 
12.4 /12.5 / 13.1 /13.3
Short-term (1 to 3 years)
FPC's Objectives
Actions and Achievements in 2022
1. Promote "circular economy" 
in each complex to implement 
reduction, reuse, and utilization 
of resources.
1. The Mailiao Complex has set a goal of reducing 
waste by 3% within three years (six-year average) to 
strengthen reuse and recycling.
2. FPC worked with cement product companies to 
submit an application to the Industrial Development 
Bureau of the Ministry of Economic Affairs to 
reuse industrial waste (calcium fluoride sludge) as 
cement product additives, and the application was 
approved in February 2022. Previously, the sludge 
waste needed to be disposed of by heat treatment, 
but it was then reused as cement product additives, 
reducing total waste by 150 tons per month.
3. FPC has worked with waste treatment companies 
to submit an application to the Ministry of Economic 
Affairs to reuse inorganic sludge. FPC has submitted 
an application to the Industrial Development Bureau 
of the Ministry of Economic Affairs in November 
2022 for waste recycling, and if approved, about 
2,000 tons of waste can be reduced per month 
through reusing.
2. Implement plans to eliminate 
white smoke visual pollution at 
the cogeneration plant.
Improvements of all six cogeneration units owned by 
FPC have been completed in April 2022.
3. The absolute reduction target of 
GHG Scope 1 and Scope 2 in 2022 
will be reduced by 2.5% compared 
with the base year (2020).
In 2021, the inventory of GHG Scope 1 and Scope 2 was 
8.604 million tons of carbon dioxide equivalent, which 
was 31,000 tons less than the absolute reduction 
target in 2020, with a reduction ratio of 0.4%, and 
efforts will continue.
4. Promote the reuse of waste and 
reduce the amount of waste 
buried in landfills.
There was 27,509 tons of direct disposal of waste in 
2022, which was a slight increase from 27,457 tons in 
2021, mainly due to the increase in inorganic sludge 
waste as a result of increased production capacity 
at the Mailiao Caustic Soda Plant. FPC is currently 
looking for a reuse plan for the inorganic sludge to 
reduce the amount of direct disposal, increase the 
recycling rate of the waste, and reduce the direct 
impact on the environment.
5. Promote source reduction of 
wastewater.
FPC continued 28 improvement plans for source 
reduction of wastewater. As of the end of 2022, 26 
improvement plans have been completed, with an 
achievement rate of 93%. The remaining improvement 
plans are currently ongoing.
6. Perform overall inspection of 
high-risk pipelines (hazardous 
fluid pipelines).
A total of 172 pipelines had to be replaced (including 
66 pipelines requiring replacement upon overall 
inspection and 106 pipelines requiring material 
improvement upon self-assessment), and the 
replacement has been completed in 2022. We will 
continue to supervise and provide guidance for all 
units to implement pipeline and RBMI inspections, so 
as to facilitate immediate repair or replacement of 
pipeline abnormalities.
7. Promote product carbon 
footprint inventory.
FPC received the Product Carbon Footprint Verification 
Statement for a total of 54 products in 2022.

FPC's Objectives
Actions and Achievements in 2022
1. Promote "circular 
economy" in each 
complex to implement 
reduction, reuse, 
and utilization of 
resources.
1. FPC is committed to promoting 
waste recycling and reducing 
the amount of direct disposal 
of waste, and aims to reduce 
the amount of direct disposal of 
non-hazardous waste by 10% in 
2025 compared with the base 
year of 2020.
2. Our 2025 reduction targets for 
various air pollutants will be 
reduced by 5% compared with 
2020, and we will achieve the 
best feasible control efficiency 
for air pollution control in all our 
manufacturing processes.
2. The absolute reduction 
target of GHG (Scope 
1 and Scope 2) in 2025 
will be reduced by 
20% compared with 
the base year.
Promote the transformation 
of coal burning to low (zero) 
carbon energy, energy-saving 
and carbon-reducing circular 
economy, increasing the use of 
renewable energy, and other 
carbon reduction measures. 
Please refer to 3.2.2 Greenhouse 
Gases Management for more 
details.
3. Promote water and 
energy conservation 
and greenhouse 
gas (GHG) emission 
reduction.
In 2022, a total of 643 energy-
saving improvement cases were 
completed, with an estimated 
GHG reduction of 108,968 tons 
CO2e/year; a total of 138 water-
saving improvement cases were 
completed, with saving of 2.345 
million liters of water in a single 
day. Please refer to 3.2.3 Energy 
Management and 3.3.3 Water 
Conservation Performance for 
complete data and statistics.
4. By 2025, 100% of all 
administrative areas 
in all complexes will 
use renewable energy.
FPC has installed its own solar 
power generation capacity, with 
456 kW already completed as of 
2022.
FPC's Objectives
Actions and Achievements in 2022
1. The absolute reduction 
target of GHG (Scope 
1 and Scope 2) in 2030 
will be reduced by 
40% compared with 
the base year, and aim 
to be carbon neutral 
by 2050.
Promote the transformation 
of coal burning to low (zero) 
carbon energy, energy-saving 
and carbon-reducing circular 
economy, increasing the use of 
renewable energy, and other 
carbon reduction measures in 
order to reach the goal of carbon 
neutral by 2050.
2. Achieve zero violation 
of environmental laws.
1. In 2022, FPC did not receive 
any industrial safety or 
environmental protection 
violation ticket issued by 
competent authorities.
2. We will continue to strengthen 
independent inspections at 
plants, source reduction and 
management, process waste 
reduction, and end control. 
Also, we will install additional 
equipment with the best 
available control technology and 
improve the effectiveness of 
pollution prevention equipment 
through AI technology.
3. Continue to promote 
a "circular economy" 
and strive toward 
achieving the "zero 
waste" objective.
FPC is committed to promoting 
waste recycling and reducing the 
amount of direct disposal of waste, 
and aims to reduce the amount of 
direct disposal of non-hazardous 
waste by 20% in 2030 compared 
with the base year of 2020.
4. Perform overall 
inspection based 
on the cycles set by 
equipment risk level.
In 2022, a total of 1,700 people 
were dispatched to conduct 
2 sessions of overall process 
inspection at 34 plants. 
Improvements were made 
on 11,518 out of the 11,521 
anomalies found in these 
inspections, demonstrating an 
overall completion rate of 99.9%. 
Improvements on the remaining 
8 anomalies are scheduled to be 
completed in the first half of 2022. 
The second stage of spot checks 
without notice was organized 
as a follow-up, with a total of 8 
sessions completed, so as to 
ensure the implementation of 
improvement at each unit.

FPC's Objectives
Actions and Achievements in 2022

2. Actively care for employees and 
offer assistance in overcoming 
difficulties to ensure talent 
retention.
1. FPC collaborated with the Teacher Chang Foundation 
by having Teacher Chang to provide regular 
consultations to employees at all complexes and to 
help solve employee problems at an early stage.
2. In 2022, a total of 59 consultations were completed. 
Please refer to 4.2.3 Employee Communication and 
Care for details.
3. Employee disabling injury 
frequency (FR) reduced to 0.15, 
disabling injury severity rate 
(SR) reduced to 0.8.
1. In 2022, the employee disabling injury frequency rate 
(FR) was 0.18, and the disabling injury severity rate 
(SR) was 4. Please refer to 4.3.1 Occupational Health 
and Safety for further details.
2. Continued building safe equipment and facilities.
3. Planed and implemented regular and automatic 
inspections of machinery and equipment.
4. Reduce energy consumption of 
office lighting.
1. Replaced all non-LED lighting at the offices with LED 
lighting.
2. As of 2022, there were 30,017 LED lamps, accounting 
for 63.6% of the total 47,222 lamps, which could 
save 128,234 kWh of electricity (about NT$384,000 
in electricity bills) and reduce carbon emissions by 
65.271 tons CO2e.

Actions and Achievements in 2022

related disability 
injury indicators 
year by year (20%).
1. Promote total inspection in each 
complex and office, and conduct in-
depth inspection and discovery of 
potential risks not identified in the 
operational procedures, including 
safety, health, process, SOP, 
machinery, electrical equipment and

practices

tons CO2e.

written forms and go green with 
paperless solutions.

electrification of 
vehicles.
1. In order to improve energy-saving 
benefits, the purchase or lease of 
official vehicles are based on energy-
saving models such as hybrid electric 
vehicles or pure electric vehicles. In 
2022, a total of 17 new/replacement 
official vehicles were purchased, 
reducing carbon emissions by 25.812 
tons CO2e per year.
2. In 2022, we subsidized employees to 
purchase or replace with 209 new 
electric scooters, reducing carbon 
emissions by 43.482 tons CO2e.

13
Special Action:  Clean Technology Research and Development to Achieve the Goal of Carbon Neutrality
Clean Technology Research and 
Development to Achieve the Goal 
of Carbon Neutrality
R&D History of Clean Technology
FPC has collaborated with academic and research institutions such as 
National Cheng Kung University (NCKU) and the Industrial Technology 
Research Institute (ITRI) to develop a technology that uses chemical 
catalysts to capture carbon dioxide (CO2) in flue gas and then purifies 
it for reuse. This technology was selected as one of the 100 most 
technologically significant new products in the 2020 R&D 100 Awards.
We have used this technology to build a chemical plant level pilot plant, 
and all raw materials (flue gas and hydrogen) and public utilities come 
from adjacent plants. The pilot plant was put into trial operation in 
December 2021, and field verification was completed in June 2022, with 
the capability to operate continuously for 24 hours. Moreover, test data 
were obtained to establish Aspen models and dynamic parameters 
were also collected, so as to serve as the basis for related tests or 
business transformation in the future. The pilot plant is the first in the 
industry in Taiwan to capture CO2 in flue gas with potassium acetate. 
It can capture about 36 tons CO2/year and convert CO2 into alkanes of 
about 13 tons/year, which can also be reused; the investment amount 
in 2022 was NT$30 million.
The project verification meeting of the Department of Industrial 
Technology, Ministry of Economic Affairs was completed on September 
14, 2022, and we were notified with a letter from the Department 
of Industrial Technology on December 2, 2022 that the project was 
concluded. Going forward, we will continue to pay close attention to the 
development of related technologies as well as explore and evaluate 
other carbon capture absorbents and hydroalkylation catalysts, in order 
to increase the capture efficiency and improve the conversion ratio of 
ethane and propane. For more information, please refer to "Capture 
and Reuse of CO2" on our Sustainable Development website.
The carbon fiber TAIRYFIL independently developed 
and produced by FPC is widely used in leisure, green 
energy, and industrial fields. As the 11
th largest 
carbon fiber manufacturer in the world, we have the 
advantage of vertical integration of light oil cracking, 
polyacrylonitrile (PAN) precursor, and carbon fiber. 
Compared with commercial products, TAIRYFIL 
carbon fiber has a higher modulus and has excellent 
compatibility with thermosetting and thermoplastic 
resins. When used in wind turbine blades, it is not 
easily deformed by rotation and has a long useful life 
with relatively high power generation efficiency. In 
response to the global green energy trend, countries 
around the world are actively promoting wind power 
generation. The sales volume of FPC's carbon fiber 
used in wind power generation exceeded 40% in 2022.
Special Action
Flue Gas Fixed Carbon Capture and Reuse Project
Application of Carbon Fiber TAIRYFIL in Wind Turbine Blades
Selected as one of the 100 most 
technologically significant new 
products in the 2020 R&D 100 Awards
Flue gas fixed carbon capture and 
reuse pilot plant

Sustainable Development Website: Capture and Reuse of CO2

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
FPC’s Goal of Carbon Neutrality by 2050
FPC actively promotes clean technology through research and 
development of technologies and materials to increase carbon 
reduction and achieve carbon neutrality. In 2022, the cumulative 
carbon reduction through clean technology research and 
development reached 74,253 tons. Additionally, FPC has officially 
joined the Science Based Targets initiative (SBTi) and passed 
the SBTi review in February 2023. FPC has adopted progressive 
carbon reduction in line with the policy and will achieve the goal of 
progressive carbon reduction through the transformation of coal 
burning to low (zero) carbon energy, energy-saving and carbon-
reducing circular economy, increasing the use of renewable 
energy, and other carbon reduction measures.
Currently, we have developed the "Flue Gas Fixed Carbon 
Capture and Reuse Project". A pilot plant has been set up with 
field verification completed and can operate continuously for 24 
hours. Through the research and development of manufacturing 
technology, it will be used as the design basis for future business 
transformation. Furthermore, we have also independently 
developed and produced "carbon fiber TAIRYFIL" to optimize 
material quality. As a raw material for high-performance 
products, it is used to provide the high-strength structure 
required for wind turbine blades in the green energy industry.
Investment amount in Clean 
Tech in 2022
NT$1.75 billion

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
1.1 Message from the Chairman
Greetings to all our partners who have supported us throughout in the development of FPC and cared for its 
growth.
2022 is a year full of challenges. The outbreak of Russia's war on Ukraine in the first quarter led to rising 
prices of energy sources, such as crude oil, natural gas, and coal, and in turn resulted in increasing prices of 
petrochemical products. FPC's consolidated revenue and profit before tax in the first half of the year both hit 
record highs compared with the same period in previous years. However, in the second half of the year, due 
to high global inflation rates and interest rate hikes in the United States and Europe, there was a decline in 
production and consumption activities, resulting in a global economic recession. This has had an inevitable 
impact on the petrochemical industry as well. Not only did demand suffer significantly, but product prices 
also dropped sharply, driving down profit margins, which led to a downturn in the petrochemical market 
in the second half of the year, making it a sharp contrast to the market boom in the first half of the year. 
Despite the challenging circumstances, all FPC employees continued to work hard together and deliver 
exceptional results, displaying perseverance and resilience. Although the annual operational performance of 
FPC declined compared with 2021, we were still able to maintain stable profit growth.
In response to the challenges of drastic changes in the international political and economic environment, 
supply chain bottlenecks, and declining demand for petrochemical products, with its sympathetic and 
forward-looking approach and years of experience in the research and development of technology and 
production, FPC has partnered with downstream partners to develop functional shoe materials and apparel 
materials that are made of fully recycled, lightweight, antibacterial, and natural materials, including fully 
recycled EVA foam shoe materials, carbon fiber safety shoes, all PP material cold-resistant clothing, etc., 
which can also be widely used in industrial operations, medical fields, consumer goods, and sports. We aim 
to achieve the goal of maintaining human health and improving the quality of life while increasing the added 
value of products and sales volume.
For almost 70 years, FPC has always adhered to the two founders' philosophy of “sustainable operation” and 
“aiming at the sovereign good”. We not only keep improving our operations but also strive to demonstrate 
our care and support for employees. In addition to being included in the "Taiwan High Compensation 100 
Index", "Taiwan Employment Creation 99 Index", and constituent stock of the "TWSE Corporate Governance 
100 Index" by the Taiwan Stock Exchange, FPC has also maintained stable profit growth. Since the Asian 
financial crisis, we have raised employee salaries year after year, so as to share our achievements with our 
hardworking and dedicated employees as well as fulfill our role in supporting thousands of families. In 2022, 
we started offering financial incentives for giving birth, including a childbirth allowance of NT$20,000 and a 
monthly childcare allowance of NT$2,000, so as to share the joy of childbirth with novice parents and reduce 
their financial burden of childcare. Meanwhile, in response to government policies, a subsidy of NT$10,000 
to NT$16,000 has been added for the purchase of (replacement with) new electric motorcycles to promote 
the use of electric vehicles for work, in an effort to contribute to a sustainable environment.
FPC has been committed to creating an excellent living environment and a better and sustainable future 
for the Earth. As of 2022, we invested a total of NT$28 billion in pollution prevention, energy conservation 
and waste reduction, greenhouse gas (GHG) reduction, and industrial safety and fire protection, achieving 
much greater results in the treatment and emissions of pollutants than the control standards set forth by 
the government. In 2022, FPC not only had zero fines for industrial safety and environmental protection but 
also was repeatedly awarded by government agencies. In addition to being awarded the Outstanding Green 
Procurement Unit by the Environmental Protection Administration and by the Department of Environmental 
Protection of Taipei City Government and the Environmental Protection Bureau Kaohsiung City Government, 
Mailiao ECH Plant and NBA Plant were honored with the Excellent Occupational Safety and Health 
Department award by the Yunlin County Government. Among them, Mailiao ECH Plant was specially honored 
with the Five-Star Award for winning for three consecutive years, showing FPC' commitment to workplace 
safety and health.

Appendix
In terms of greenhouse gas reduction, FPC’s carbon reduction strategy passed the review by the Science-
Based Reduction Target Initiative (SBTi) in December 2022. The greenhouse gas (Scope 1 and 2) emissions 
in 2021 have been verified by a third-party, with a confirmed total of 8.604 million tons, representing a 
decrease of 0.4% compared with the 2022 absolute reduction target of 31,000 tons. To improve reduction 
and continue to promote water and energy conservation, in 2022 alone, we conserved 3,789 tons of water 
per day and reduced an additional 136 thousand tons of GHG emissions per year. There are 1,179 projects 
that are continuously carried out and it is estimated that the daily consumption of water will save another 
8,202 tons of water, and the annual GHG emissions will be reduced by another 389 thousand tons. According 
to the 2022 assessment results announced by the Carbon Disclosure Project (CDP), an international 
environmental assessment index, FPC was given an A- rating in both climate change assessment and 
water resource assessment and ranked among the best for internationally renowned chemical companies 
in consecutive years. Such performance has confirmed FPC's significant results in energy conservation, 
emission reduction, and circular economy in response to climate change.
To implement industrial safety management, prevent occupational disasters, and protect labor safety 
and health, in addition to continuously promoting the inspection of process equipment, implementing 
standard operating procedures (SOP), management of change (MOC), and process hazard analysis (PHA), 
and strengthening the inspection of machinery and equipment for improvement, mobile cameras also 
have been installed in recent years at the domestic and foreign factory construction sites to strengthen the 
control of work progress and assist supervisors and contractors in proper industrial safety management. 
Furthermore, a construction site safety image recognition system has been developed to set up electronic 
fences using AI and image recognition technology. It has been applied to personnel control at construction 
sites, safety belt warning, and high-risk area management to ensure 24-hour monitoring, prevent 
occupational accidents, and establish a friendly and healthy workplace.
Looking ahead to a new year, in view of the global ESG transformation, FPC will deepen corporate 
governance, integrate sustainable values into various business strategies, and work towards the United 
Nations Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs). Also, in response to the post-pandemic trends of health 
care, technological innovation, and economic development, we are committed to research and development 
of environmentally friendly and medical-grade products, such as fully recycled plastics, anti-adhesive 
composite rubber particles, biodegradable and green plastics, so as to accelerate product transformation 
and create multiple values. Furthermore, we will continue to promote strategies such as low-carbon energy 
transformation, energy conservation and carbon reduction, circular economy, and use of renewable energy, 
strengthen the risk control of climate change, complete the carbon footprint inventory of major products, 
and collaborate with upstream and downstream supply chain partners to promote ESG transformation, so as 
to ensure we are moving towards the 2050 Carbon Neutrality goal and fulfilling our sustainable commitment.
Last but not least, we will further deepen AI development and research, strengthen industry-academia-
research collaboration, seek forward-looking technology transfer or cooperative development, and create 
a new blueprint for future development. We look forward to strengthening FPC's business resilience 
through innovative and adaptable business strategies and making full preparation for the next wave of 
petrochemical industry growth, so that we can continue to break through difficulties in the downturn and 
maintain stable profit growth. As a good corporate citizen, we will contribute our best efforts to create a 
sustainable future and work towards the common good of society.
Formosa Plastics Corporation
Chairman
2023

1.2 About FPC
1.2.1 Management Philosophy
As a member of the Formosa Plastics Group (FPG), Formosa Plastics Corporation (FPC) has undergone 
nearly 70 years of development based on the management philosophy of the late founders, Mr. Wang 
Yung-Ching and Mr. Wang Yung-Tsai, who always emphasized and 
demonstrated the spirit of “Diligence, Perseverance, Frugality and 
Trustworthiness; To Aim at the Sovereign Good; Perpetual Business 
Operation; and Dedication to the Society.” For more information on 
the founders of FPG, please refer to FPG's official website.

website.

1.4 Identification of Material Issues
By analyzing material issues, FPC can understand the issues of concern to the stakeholders and evaluate 
the impact of these issues as a reference for the preparation of this Report.
1.4.1 Analytical Process for Material Issues
3-1
Identiﬁcation
7 Types of Important 
Stakeholders
Through discussions between the 
editorial team of this Report and 
heads of various departments, 
this Report referenced the five 
major principles of the AA1000 
Stakeholder Engagement Standard 
(SES) to identify 7 main groups of 
stakeholders.
Collection of Corporate 
Impacts
99 Impacts
After referencing the Sustainability 
Accounting Standards Board (SASB), 
the Task Force on Climate-related 
Financial Disclosures (TCFD), the 
Sustainable Development Best 
Practice Principles for TWSE/TPEx 
Listed Companies, the ISO 26000 
Guidance on Social Responsibility, 
international ratings of industry 
issues, the United Nations 
Sustainable Development Goals 
(SDGs), domestic and foreign 
industry issues, global trends and 
issues, as well as media reports, 
the editorial team of this Report 
identified and determined 99 positive 
and negative corporate impacts.
Grouping of Corporate 
Impacts into 
Sustainability Issues
26 Sustainability Issues

by the consultant team, the impacts 
were grouped into sustainability 
issues according to topics. Then, 
through discussions between 
the core members of the ESG 
Promotion Task Force and external 
consultants, 26 sustainability issues 
were identified.

Explanation on the adjustments of material topics disclosed in the current year
To focus on the issues of concern more accurately to stakeholders, the Sustainable Development 
Promotion Team of FPC reviewed the materiality analysis process this year by referencing domestic and 
foreign industry trends, clarifying the significance of the sustainability issues, and adjusting the scope of 
materiality as appropriate. Adjustments to the material topics this year are described below:

Management
Medium

Increased
In response to high greenhouse gas emissions of the 
chemical industry and increasingly stringent government 
regulations, FPC has established the goal of achieving 
carbon neutrality by 2050. It will continue to promote 
carbon reduction strategies, improve energy, and 
resource efficiency, and reduce carbon emissions to 
respond to stakeholder concerns.

Management
High
Low
This is the most important topic for the top three 
stakeholders of FPC, namely employees, suppliers, and 
contractors. FPC continues to enhance corporate ethics 
by formulating and complying with the code of ethics and 
internal control as well as strictly prohibiting corruption 
and competition.

maintenance, and various actions to improve industrial 
safety.

determined to be an issue outside the matrix.
1.4.3 Identification of Impacts and Value Chain
Following the five-stage value chain identified in 2018, FPC has further analyzed the material topics 
corresponding to each stage of value chain and assessed the types of stakeholders affected. To identify 
and effectively manage the impacts caused by material topics, FPC divided them into “Cause”, “Contribute 
To”, and “Directly Linked To” impacts based on the degree of involvement in order to effectively manage 
the impact of major issues and improve the efficiency of communication with stakeholders.

Note 1: Level of Financial Impact: "High" refers to a financial impact greater than NT$10 billion, "Medium High" refers to a financial impact between 
NT$1 billion and NT$10 billion, "Medium" refers to a financial impact between NT$100 million and NT$1 billion, "Medium Low" refers to a 
financial impact between NT$10 million and NT$100 million, and "Low" refers to a financial impact less than NT$10 million.
Note 2: “Cause” means that an organization causes a negative impact if its activities on their own result in the impact; “Contribute To” means that an 
organization contributes to a negative impact if its activities lead, facilitate, or incentivize another entity to cause the impact; “Directly Linked 
To” means that even if an organization does not cause or contribute to a negative impact, its operations, products, or services may be directly 
linked to a negative impact by its business relationships.

Investment in Formosa Smart Energy Tech Corp.
In response to global carbon-reduction initiatives, the development of renewable energy and electric 
vehicles, and government investment in energy transition, in 2022, FPC, along with Nan Ya Plastics 
Corporation (NPC), Formosa Chemicals & Fibre Corporation (FCFC), Formosa Petrochemical Corporation 
(FPCC), and Formosa Biomedical Technology Corporation (FBC), jointly invested NT$7 billion and integrated 
group resources to establish Formosa Smart Energy Tech Corp., making every effort to promote and 
deploy key new energy technologies in terms of four major aspects, namely energy conservation, energy 
storage, new energy, and recycling and reuse:
Energy Conservation: We strive to increase energy efficiency by bettering production processes and improve 
energy-saving and carbon-reducing technologies. We will not only develop energy-saving and smart energy 
recycling systems for different energy-use sectors (including homes, offices, and manufactories) but also invest in 
research and development of energy-saving management technologies for balancing peak and off-peak hours of 
electricity use.
Energy Storage: We plan to produce batteries for the UPS Emergency Backup Power Supply, provide energy 
storage systems for home, commercial, and industrial use, employ automated frequency coordination (AFC) 
services, and build grid energy storage stations. Furthermore, we will collaborate with domestic and foreign 
vehicle manufacturers on the development of automotive battery modules for electric vehicles, electric buses, and 
electric commercial vehicles.
New Energy: We are developing smart grid control systems to improve the efficiency of green energy, diversifying 
energy creation sectors, and increasing the proportion of green energy usage.
Recycling and Reuse: We are developing lithium battery recycling technology and carbon capture technology as 
well as deploying technologies for water resource recycling, activation and reuse of speciality chemicals (such as 
industrial catalysts), and precious metal recycling.

In order to assist the industry in resource exchange and integration, act as a bridge of communication 
with the government, and promote the sustainable development of the industry, FPC actively participates 
in various industry associations. In 2022, FPC was a member of 19 external associations and served as a 
director, supervisor, or representative of such associations; in particular, Chairman Mr. Jason Lin served 
as the chairman of Taiwan Synthetic Resins Manufacturers Association. For more information on FPC's 
participation in external associations, please refer to our Sustainable Development website.

Management

Monitoring
Internal Audit Management
Results in 2022
 
◈Performed monthly audits on various items according to the annual audit plan, 
monitored the improvement results of items that failed audits, and submitted 
audit reports to independent directors for review every month. In 2022, audits 
were conducted on 59 items, and the audit completion rate was 100%.
 
◈Convened Board meetings at least once every quarter to report the internal audit 
status to the Board of Directors, and approved the audit plan for the following year 
at the end of the year.
 
◈The internal audit officer and independent directors communicated individually on 
the audit results of internal control, revisions of the internal control system, and 
audit plans at least once a year.
 
◈To establish sound mechanisms for the handling and disclosure of material inside 
information and prevent improper information disclosures, FPC has formulated 
the Procedures for Handling Material Inside Information upon resolution by the 
Board of Directors on November 10, 2022. We require our directors, managerial 
officers, and employees to exercise the due care and fiduciary duty of a good 
administrator, act in good faith when performing their duties, and treat material 
inside information of FPC with confidentiality. Additionally, to ensure material 
inside information of FPC is timely, accurate, and complete, prior to any public 
disclosure of such information, the responsible unit in charge must formulate 
drafts and submit the version to be released for review as well as assess and 
examine whether it complies with applicable laws and regulations regarding the 
disclosure of material inside information.

ESG Risk
Management Policies
Guide FPC's long-term business 
strategy and supervise FPC to 
fulfill its management obligations 
to achieve sustainable operation.
On December 17, 2020, the Board of Directors approved the 
"Regulations Governing Risk Management". Among them, the risk 
management categories focuses on three major topics: environment (E), 
society (S) and corporate governance (G). Risk items including strategy, 
operation, finance, hazard, information security, regulatory compliance, 
climate change, energy management, water resource management and 
so on are identified according to the three risk categories of preventable 
risk, strategic risk and external risk.
Report the implementation of risk management to the Board of 
Directors at least once every year, with the most recent reporting date 
being June 9, 2022.

Remuneration Policy for Directors of the Company
The remuneration of FPC’s directors and managers are first submitted to the Remuneration Committee 
for resolution and then submitted to the Board of Directors for further discussion and approval. For the 
remuneration of directors, in accordance with Article 28 of the Company's Articles of Incorporation, the 
Board of Directors is authorized to make decisions based on the extent of the directors' participation in 
the Company's operations and the value of their contributions, and with reference to the usual level of 
payments in the industry. However, the independent directors and director Ralph Ho receive fixed monthly 
remuneration and travel expenses based on their actual attendance at the board meetings. The rest of 
the directors only receive travel expenses based on their actual attendance at the board meetings, and 
no variable compensation is paid. For information on directors' remuneration in 2022, please refer to 
"Remuneration of General Directors and Independent Directors" in the annual report.
The remuneration of the President and Vice President is paid in accordance with Article 36 of the Company's 
Articles of Association. The fixed monthly salary is based on the salary adjustment standard of all employees 
every year. The Chairman will assess and evaluate comprehensively the overall performance (including 
financial and non-financial indicators, see the table below) and the achievement of the "Annual Performance 
Targets" according to the responsibilities of each managerial position and then submit an adjustment 
proposal to the Remuneration Committee. For information on the managerial officers' remuneration in 2022, 
please refer to the “The President and Vice President’s Remuneration Policy" in the annual report.

(2) Remuneration Committee
The Remuneration Committee is composed of 4 independent directors and holds at least 2 meetings every 
year. During these meetings, remuneration policies and systems for directors and managerial officers are 
evaluated, and recommendations are submitted to the Board of Directors for deliberation, so as to prevent 
directors and managerial officers from engaging in conduct that exceeds the risk appetite of FPC due to 
remuneration policies.

(3) Audit Committee
The Audit Committee is composed of 4 independent directors and holds at least 2 meetings every year. The 
main purpose of establishing this committee is to supervise the fair expression of financial statements, 
the appointment (dismissal), competence, independence and performance of CPAs, the effective 
implementation of internal control, compliance with the relevant laws and regulations, and the control of 
existing or potential risks to FPC.

2.2.2 Promotion of Corporate Sustainability
FPC has appointed Chairman Mr. Jason Lin to serve as the convener as well as President Mr. Wen-
Bee Kuo and Senior Vice President Mr. Jerry Lin to serve as the deputy conveners of the Sustainable 
Development Promotion Team. They are responsible for developing sustainable development strategies, 
supervising the performance of these strategies, and promoting operations such as social responsibility 
and risk management.
The order of the themes and issues of this Report were decided in a meeting at the beginning of 2022 by 
the President's Office, Safety and Health Department, Accounting Department, Mailiao Administration 
Department, Kaohsiung Administration Department, and members of the “Sustainable Development 
Promotion Task Force.” The content of this Report was first compiled and submitted to the convener and 
the deputy convener before being reported to the Board of Directors at least once every year in order to 
ensure that the issues disclosed in this Report are in line with the needs of stakeholders.

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
2.2.3 Risk management
 
 Risk management 
For each identified operational risk, FPC has designated a risk management unit in charge of assessing 
and reviewing the risk and developing relevant response measures in hopes of effectively strengthening 
the soundness of business operations. For more 
information, please refer to our Sustainable 
Development website.
Sustainable Development Website: Risk Management
FPC’s Current Risk Management Approach
Legal Basis
The Board of Directors approved the "Regulations Governing Risk Management" 
and formulated FPC's risk management policy, explaining risk management 
procedures such as risk identification, risk measurement, risk control and 
supervision, risk reporting and disclosure, risk performance management and 
improvement, etc.
Sustainable Development Promotion Team
According to FPC’s Regulations Governing Risk Management, the scope of risks 
includes:
Production and marketing meetings are held monthly, and business 
performance meetings, safety and environmental performance meetings, 
energy conservation and emission reduction circular economy review meetings, 
project review meetings, and regular ESG implementation progress reports are 
held quarterly, in order to regularly review operating conditions, determine 
potential risks and opportunities, and promptly adjust risk response strategies.
The implementation of risk management is reported to the Board of Directors 
at least once every year. The report includes the focus of risk management, risk 
assessment and corresponding mitigation measures to ensure the integrity, 
rationality and optimization of risk management. The most recent reporting 
date was June 9, 2022.
Responsible
Unit
Management 
Scope
Operations
Strategic risks: include changes in the overall economic environment, changes 
in the industrial market, changes in technological development, changes in 
policies and regulations, changes in competitors, etc.
Operational risks: include production operations, supply chain, fluctuations in 
raw materials and product prices, customer sales, intellectual property rights, 
human resources, corporate image, taxation, legal proceedings, and other 
risks due to internal operational factors.
Financial risks: include market risks arising from fluctuations in interest rates 
and currency exchange rates, credit transaction risks, liquidity risks due to 
inability to liquidate assets or obtain adequate funding or due to inadequate 
market depth, etc.
Hazard risks: include typhoons, earthquakes, floods, infectious diseases, 
interruptions of utilities such as water and electricity, wars or terrorist 
attacks, social unrest, strikes, industrial safety accidents, and other risks due 
to natural disasters or major hazardous events.
Other risks: include other risks such as information security, climate change, 
legal compliance, changes in management rights, etc.
Additionally, in terms of environment (E), society (S), and corporate governance (G), 
risks are identified based on three categories, namely preventable risks, strategy 
risks, and external risks.

Risk Management Strategy
Responsible Unit
Results in 2022
1. The Water Shortage Emergency Response Team 
is established to oversee the current status 
of water sources at each production complex 
and propose projects and R&D of technologies 
that promote zero wastewater discharge 
and rainwater recycling, so as to improve the 
efficiency of water resource recycling, strengthen 
the adaptability to changes, and reduce the risk 
of water shortage.
2. Enhance water conservation management 
measures (such as reducing non-production 
water use and ensuring the normal operation of 
wastewater recycling and reuse facilities), expand 
the rainwater collection area at each production 
complex, and accelerate the completion of 
various water conservation improvement 
projects.
3. Since the desalination plant in Mailiao started 
operations in 2023, about 100,000 tons of 
water has been produced every day, which 
helps mitigate the water supply stress at the 
Mailiao complex. We also continue to review 
various water conservation improvements and 
wastewater recycling and reuse technologies 
(such as the algae treatment system of the 
Biotechnology Center at National Cheng Kung 
University) to reduce water supply.
4. Until the completion of the water conservation 
improvement projects at each production 
complex, if water shortages continue to develop, 
evaluations will be performed based on factors 
such as the water consumption of each complex 
and the current profit per ton of water used, and 
priority will be given to reducing production at 
complexes with lower profit per unit of water.

Risk Management Strategy
Responsible Unit
Results in 2022
1. In order to mitigate climate change, FPC has 
formulated short-, medium-, and long-term 
response strategies for 2025, 2030, and 2050 in 2021. 
In the future, we will achieve the goal of progressive 
carbon reduction through the transformation of coal 
burning to low (zero) carbon energy, energy-saving 
and carbon-reducing circular economy, increasing 
the use of renewable energy, and other carbon 
reduction measures.
2. We promote the integration of energy and resources 
across the complexes/Company and hold monthly 
energy conservation and carbon reduction promotion 
meetings to review the implementation progress and 
results as well as to improve our energy conservation 
and carbon reduction technologies.
3. We research and develop green products, enhance 
the weather resistance and reusability of products, 
reduce carbon emissions in the production process, 
and extend product life cycles.
Safety and Health 
Department, 
Safety, Health and 
Environment Center
In 2021, the inventory of GHG 
Scope 1 and Scope 2 was 8.604 
million tons of carbon dioxide 
equivalent, which was 31,000 tons 
less than the absolute reduction 
target in 2020, with a reduction 
ratio of 0.4%. The emission 
intensity decreased from 6,205.40 
tons of CO2e/NT$100 million in 
2020 to 4,084.04 tons of CO2e/
NT$100 million in 2021.
Energy Management
Risk Management Strategy
Responsible Unit
Results in 2022
1. Strengthen energy conservation management 
measures, such as reducing the amount of steam 
used in the production process, improving the power 
efficiency of production equipment, increasing 
combustion equipment efficiency, etc.
2. Deploy AI applications to all production complexes, 
and use simulation software to simulate optimal 
production parameters, improve the performance of 
the distillation tower, and reduce steam consumption.
3. Continuously review how to improve the performance 
of rotating equipment, including replacement of the 
materials of water tower fan blades with carbon 
fibers, magnetic levitation blowers, magnetic 
levitation chillers, magnetized energy-saving rods for 
boilers, etc.
4. Until the completion of the improvement projects 
at each production complex, if energy shortages 
continue to develop, evaluations will be performed 
based on factors such as the energy consumption 
of each complex and the current profit per unit 
of energy consumed, and priority will be given to 
reducing production at complexes with lower profit 
per unit of energy consumed.
President's Office 
at Complex, 
Management Unit at 
President's Office
In 2022, a total of 126 steam-
saving improvement cases 
were completed, with saving of 
32.82 tons/hour. A total of 512 
electricity-saving improvement 
cases were completed, with 
saving of 5,300 kWh/hour.
Risk Management Strategy
Responsible Unit
Results in 2022
1. Design and build plants with best available 
technology (BAT) and best available control 
technology (BACT), and promote measures to 
reduce waste gas emissions and volatile organic 
compounds (VOCs), control odors, etc.
2. Strengthen the control over leaks of equipment 
components at all plants and monitor air 
quality in real-time through fourier-transform 
infrared spectroscopy (FTIR) analysis at the FTIR 
stations established at the Renwu, Mailiao, and 
Linyuan complexes, with three additional mobile 
spectrometers inside the plants.
3. Air pollution controls and improvements are 
continuously implemented to prevent air pollution 
incidents, in hopes of achieving the goal of “zero 
pollution”.
Safety and Health 
Department

(0% anomaly rate) in the process.

of petrochemical process 
equipment: In 2022, 21,664 units 
were streamlined, reducing VOCs 
emissions by 2.734 tons/year as 
well as saving inspection costs of 
NT$1,213 thousand/year and air 
pollution fees of NT$96 thousand/
year, with a total cost reduction of 
NT$1,309 thousand/year.

Risk Management Strategy
Responsible Unit
Results in 2022
1. FPC carries out waste reduction through three 
major measures, including source management, 
process reduction and end-of-pipe disposal, so the 
waste directly disposed of is the actual waste.
2. We are committed to promoting the reuse of waste 
and reducing the amount of landfills.
Safety and Health 
Department
1. Waste reduction during 
production processes: The waste 
materials generated during 
production stages, such as the 
by-products (previously disposed 
of as waste) derived from the 
production process of U-CAL 
were recycled and reused to 
produce TAICAL.
2. End disposal (reuse): FPC worked 
with cement product companies 
to submit an application to the 
Industrial Development Bureau 
of the Ministry of Economic 
Affairs to reuse industrial waste 
(calcium fluoride sludge) as 
cement product additives, and 
the application was approved 
in February 2022. Previously, 
the sludge waste needed to be 
disposed of by heat treatment, 
but it was then reused as cement 
product additives, reducing total 
waste by 150 tons per month.

Policy 
Commitments
 
◈When engaging in commercial activities, directors, managers, and employees 
of FPC shall not directly or indirectly offer, promise to offer, request or accept 
any improper benefits, nor commit unethical acts.
 
◈FPC complies with the Company Act, the Securities and Exchange Act, and 
other laws and regulations related to business practices.
 
◈FPC ensures that its employees strictly abide by the policies for preventing 
conflicts of interest and comply with non-competition clauses to avoid any 
work-related conflicts of interests.

Appendix
(1) Professional and Independent Internal Auditing System
FPC has established the independent Audit Office under the Board of Directors. Each year, the Audit Office 
is responsible to carry out independent auditing and supervision of business functions to ensure their 
management efficiency, and reduce operating risks. No major deficiency was found in all 59 audit items in 
2022. For more information on internal control mechanism, please refer to our Sustainable Development 
website.
For more information on the internal audit organization and its 
operation, please refer to "Audit System" on FPC's official website.
(2) Ethical Corporate Management and Anti-Corruption Policies
FPC has implemented a stringent code of ethics to prevent trade secret leaks, misconduct, malpractice 
or misappropriation of funds, as well as behavior which violates gender equality at work. For more 
information on concrete measures, please refer 
to "Ethical Corporate Management & Conduct" 
on FPC's official website.

New activated carbon recycling/
regeneration system
1. Activated carbon adsorption systems are often used 
in waste gas and wastewater treatment. After the 
adsorption is saturated, the cost of activated carbon 
treatment and cleaning can be very expensive.
2. The new activated carbon recycling/regeneration 
system with automatic control can not only improve the 
working environment and reduce the cost of regular 
replacement of activated carbon but also achieve the 
goals of waste reduction and resource recycling.
Biodegradable PP 
1. Biodegradable PP raw materials can be 
applied to extrusion grade disposable 
products, such as lunch boxes, water cups, 
food packaging bags, etc.
2. It has passed the first phase of the BSI PAS9017 
certification and is currently undergoing the 
second and third phases of certification. FPC 
is actively promoting it and has sold a small 
amount to lunch box manufacturers for testing.
Super absorbent resin (SAP) 
for adult diapers
1. We have partnered with Japanese customers 
to develop super absorbent resin (SAP) for 
adult diapers with high absorption and urine 
conductivity.
2. Product development and market trial 
sales have been completed. The product 
performance is better than that of Japanese 
products. We will continue to collect feedback 
from consumers for improvement.
Post-consumer recycled PP plastics (PCR)
1. In line with our ESG commitments and company 
policies, we have developed post-consumer recycled 
PP plastics (PCR), namely YUNGSOX product 
numbers RP1040, RP3401, and RP4304, which are 
mainly used in the production of woven bags, daily 
necessities, pallets, car pumps, etc.
2. We initially tested the woven bags made of PCR 
RP1040 mixed with pure PP materials, and a 
customer used RP3401 in producing storage boxes 
to reduce resource waste and achieve sustainable 
development.

Non-toxic Safety Product Certiﬁcation
FPC is committed to reducing hazardous formulas, improving waste reduction 
in processes, and developing green products. With our products registered and 
certified in accordance with relevant laws and regulations, we are moving toward a 
manufacturer of non-toxic, eco-friendly products and renewable energy.
In 2022, the solar encapsulation film-grade ethylene vinyl acetate copolymer (EVA) 
obtained not only the ROHS certification but also the Restricted Substance List (RSL) 
certification of international sports goods manufacturers such as NIKE, NB, and 
ADIDAS as well as the European Union's Plastics Regulation (EU NO.10) certification. 
Additionally, the REACH pre-registration for solid sodium hydroxide in UK and Turkey 
has been completed in 2022, and we are expecting to obtain the REACH certificate by 
the end of 2023.
 
Green Materials
Circular Economy with FPC, Turning Waste into Gold - Fully Recyclable EVA Foam Flip-ﬂops
Motivation for Development
 As a leading supplier of innovative materials, the research and development team of 
FPC has successfully developed ethylene vinyl acetate (EVA) foam materials through 
long-term partnerships with Der Cheng Tannery Co., Ltd., a top manufacturer 
of running slippers, and King Steel Machinery Co., Ltd., a leading manufacturer 
of machinery for shoe production. In 2022, a total of 3 patent applications were 
filed, one of which has been approved in October, and the other two are still being 
reviewed.
 Upon testing, shoe materials made of FPC’s green and eco-friendly EVA foam material 
(EF-FOAM) are soft, resilient, and light weight. Most importantly, it represents our 
value of sustainable recycling. Being 100% recyclable, it is one of the key products for 
FPC to build a green supply chain and promote sustainability.
 FPC’s green and eco-friendly EVA foam material (EF-FOAM) has been 
officially showcased at the Germany K Show in October 2022.
Product Application
 Shoe materials
 The annual sales volume of fully recyclable EVA foam flip-
flops is 2 million pairs, and the annual sales of EVA is 
estimated to increase by 500 tons, which reduces not only the 
amount of waste disposal but also carbon emissions by 1,100 
tons per year.

Plant in 2020 to accelerate the development of AI technology. AI educational training and competitions are 
held internally, and an AI exchange platform, AI proposal reward system (after being approved by the AI review

the evaluation of AI performance were set up. Relevant AI technologies are introduced externally, seeking AI

FPC’s AI development mainly focuses on the five major aspects of "production and sales optimization, quality 
assurance, process optimization, intelligent maintenance, and industrial safety and environmental protection" 
in order to achieve the goals of ensuring customer delivery, improving product quality, reducing production 
costs, avoiding process abnormalities, and improving the working environment in the plant. Our future

Case
Production and Sales Optimization - E-Business Platform
Existing operational defects
The traditional processing procedure 
is that customers place orders, 
inquire about prices, and negotiate 
delivery dates directly with sales 
representatives, which requires a lot 
of paperwork and a complex workflow 
and reduces work efficiency.
Development of AI
An e-commerce platform is 
established to disclose product 
information and allow customers to 
place orders online. Also, appropriate 
delivery dates are calculated using AI 
production scheduling models, which 
reduces paperwork processing and 
alleviates the workload of sales staff.
Beneﬁts after going online
1. Reduce 80% operating time for staff.
2. Access order information in real-time to reduce unnecessary 
product transfer times.
3. Integrate production, sales, and inventory to strengthen 
management and increase order delivery rate by 12%.
4. Provide quality customer service:
(1) Provide product information for 
customers to quickly understand how to 
use products.
(2) Provide convenient purchasing services 
through online inquiry, quotation, and 
ordering.
(3) Effectively grasp the status of purchase 
progress and inform customers 
proactively of the status of their orders.
(4) Use historical purchase records to 
provide customers with historical 
purchase status, including unit price, 
quantity, and purchase time.

60
2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
Quality Assurance - Automatic Particle Size Control for Super Absorbent Resin (SAP)
Existing operational defects
According to the characteristics of SAP products, different products require different particle 
sizes. In the past, the thickness of each product was controlled by manually setting the grinding 
parameters, but this method relied heavily on the experience of operators, and there were two major 
pain points:
1. When there was a slight disturbance in the process (such as a variation of raw materials), on-site 
operators might not be able to find it in time.
2. The adjustment of grinding parameters was mainly based on trial and error, which did not 
guarantee optimum results right away, therefore reducing production efficiency.
Development of AI
An automatic grinding control system has been established by integrating statistical process control 
(SPC) with machine learning models. SPC is used to determine whether the production process 
is unstable based on real-time data, and then machine learning models provide the best grinding 
parameters for the system based on the most similar scenario from historical data.
Beneﬁts after going online
1. When the production process is unstable, the automation will intervene 8 hours in advance to 
stabilize the system and therefore reduce manual processing and monitoring workloads.
2. Reduce the production rate of SAP fine powder and improve product quality.

Process Optimization - Optimization of Polyvinyl Chloride (PVC) Polymerization Tank Reaction Time
Existing operational defects
PVC polymerization is an exothermic reaction. In the past, the amount of catalyst added was 
adjusted manually by the operator. As it was difficult to predict precisely the heat release amount, 
in order to avoid incorrect reaction, the amount of catalyst added was adjusted incrementally and 
gradually, resulting in a time-consuming and energy-consuming process due to the heat removal 
capacity of the polymerization tank not being fully utilized during the polymerization process.
Development of AI
FPC has incorporated chemical kinetics into the process simulation technology to develop AI models 
to predict the heat release of the reaction, automatically correct the catalyst efficiency parameters, 
as well as calculate the optimal catalyst combination and addition time points, so as to improve the 
overall reaction rate, maximize the heat removal capacity of the polymerization tank, shorten the 
reaction time, and increase the product volume while preventing unnecessary energy consumption.
Beneﬁts after going online
Taking the most profitable products S-65D and S-70 as an example, the average reaction time 
can be shortened by 40 and 15 minutes respectively, improving the production rate of the PVC 
polymerization tank. Also, the production volume can be increased by about 20 tons per day, saving 
power consumption by nearly 483,000 kWh and reducing carbon emissions by about 290 tons Co2e 
per year.

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
Case
Smart Maintenance - Pump Cavitation Warning
Existing operational defects
When the pump lubricant (or process fluid) polymerizes, the inlet filter cartridge will be blocked. 
Before the low current protection system triggers an alarm, the pump will still go through early 
stages of cavitation, causing damage to internal components (bearings, shafts, and impellers).
Development of AI
Current signal analysis and AI algorithms are integrated to establish an AI model for cavitation 
classification during the initial stage. The data center server regularly sends the pump current signal 
back to the AI model for analysis and failure warning and then sends the analysis results to the 
maintenance personnel in real time through a communication software to control equipment failures.
Beneﬁts after going online
Pump cavitation used to occur about 15 times on average every year. After the implementation of the 
AI warning model, cavitation can be detected during the initial stage to prevent severe equipment 
damage, prolong the service life of equipment components, and save maintenance costs.

Case
Industrial Safety Management - Electronic Fencing
Existing operational defects
When construction is taking place at a production plant, it is necessary for supervisors to monitor 
whether there are workers entering dangerous areas without proper authorization. However, the 
monitoring is extremely time-consuming, and supervisors cannot work continuously without breaks, 
which causes concerns about industrial safety.
Development of AI
The electronic fencing system can allow supervisors to delineate dangerous areas, utilize cameras 
and AI monitoring models to manage dangerous zones, as well as alert on-site staff to avoid 
industrial accidents.
Beneﬁts after going online
Effectively prevent industrial safety accidents and reduce the burden of supervisors.

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
Case
Environmental Management - Real-time COD Monitoring of Wastewater for 
Epichlorohydrin (ECH) Saponiﬁcation Reactor
Existing operational defects
The COD inspection of ECH saponification wastewater adopts the potassium dichromate reflux 
method, and the inspection takes about 4 to 6 hours. Abnormal wastewater COD value cannot be 
accessed in real time.
Development of AI
We have established an AI model based on the process parameters of the ECH reaction to predict 
the COD value in real time and adjust the process parameters accordingly, so that the COD value can 
be maintained within the control range (3,000 ppm) on the premise that the production conversion 
rate is met. 
Beneﬁts after going online
The average COD value of wastewater is reduced by about 59 ppm (2,227 →2,168 ppm).
(4) Intellectual Property Management
To facilitate the management of R&D projects such as new products and new technologies, FPC has 
established the "Regulations Governing Research and Development Management" and set up related 
computer operations; in addition, FPC has specified incentives for R&D and patent authorization 
concerning key products in the "Regulations Governing Incentives for Research and Development 
Achievements Among R&D Personnel," with the aim of encouraging R&D personnel to engage in 
innovative development and actively conduct research, thereby enhancing our competitiveness. On the 
other hand, FPC requires all employees to submit the "Statement of Respect for Intellectual Property 
Rights" and conducts training on laws and regulations related to intellectual property rights, so as 
to enhance employees' awareness of intellectual property rights. In 2022, the number of valid patent 
certificates granted was 40, making the cumulative number of valid patents 250. For more information, 
please refer to "Intellectual Property Rights" 
on our Sustainable Development website.

Customer Feedback and Response
To solve customers' inquiries and needs in a timely manner, FPC has set up "Contact Us" on the official 
website. Customers may also make inquiries or comments by calling us or writing to an e-mail address 
listed on the official website. In case of return of goods and refunds, customers may express their 
feedback to sales representatives. The sales representatives will then fill out the "Customer Complaint 
Form" to handle the cases and process return of goods, allowances or refunds. In 2022, a total of 24 
customer complaints have been received, all of which have been properly handled and closed, and 
customers' opinions were responded to in a timely manner. 
 
  Information Protection
FPC has established the "Regulations Governing Personal Information 
Management," which requests all relevant departments to list personal 
data management as a self-inspection item. Only authorized personnel 
are allowed to check employee or customer information. Any personnel 
intending to get access to such information due to business needs must 
sign the "Application Form for Personal Information Collection, Processing 
and Use," while verification has to be carried out to ensure that such 
an application complies with the regulations before the personnel can 
access such information. No violations related to information privacy were 
reported by clients in 2022.
2.4.2 Customer Satisfaction Survey
To fulfill the requirements of ISO 9001 regarding quality commitment to customers and show FPC's focus 
on customer satisfaction, a satisfaction survey is conducted among FPC's domestic and foreign customers 
at least once a year. The survey questions are further modified based on the issues or areas of concern 
that customers have previously expressed. 
According to the customer satisfaction 
survey in 2022, FPC's overall performance 
was 4.4 points, with only two items 
in "product price" falling short of 
customers’ expectations. This was 
mainly due to the increase in costs of 
raw materials, which subsequently 
led to an increase in product prices, 
thus causing its score to be slightly 
lower than that of other indicators. 
The overall satisfaction scores from 
2016 to 2022 were higher than the 
benchmark of "satisfied" (4 points). 
FPC incorporates customer feedback 
and suggestions into the operation 
policies, and strives to continuously 
improve the professional competencies 
and service attitude of the sales 
representatives and technicians to 
better meet customer expectations.

3.1.1 Environment, Health and 
Safety Management 
FPC has established the Safety and Health Department to be responsible for issuing guidelines on 
overall safety, health, environment, and fire policies for FPC and implementing external operations. It is 
supervised and assessed by the Safety, Health and Environment Center under the Group Administration 
Office. Furthermore, safety and health departments have been established at each complex to promote 
safe, health, environment, and fire management.
In addition, we hold regular safety, health and environmental review meetings every year to achieve the goal 
of zero disaster in safety, health and health management and zero pollution in environmental protection.

GRI 2-27
Policy 
Commitments
 
◈Environmental protection and pollution prevention are the responsibilities of 
every company. FPC strictly abides by environmental laws and regulations to 
achieve the goal of zero penalty within five years, thereby fulfilling our vision of 
corporate sustainability.
 
◈Upholding the business philosophy of balancing “safety, health, and 
environment and economic development”, FPC implements the “Safety, Health 
and Environment Policy” approved by the Chairman and strives to strengthen 
communication with nearby residents. For more policy information, please 
refer to FPC's official website.
Management 
Approach and 
Performance 
Monitoring
Environmental Protection Audit
 
◈FPC has established the “Regulations Governing Supervision and Management 
of Environmental Protection”, which stipulates that employees at all levels shall 
fulfill environmental protection-related duties, and that the Safety and Health 
Department, the Safety and Health Team at each division, and environmental 
protection personnel at each complex and department shall conduct 
environmental protection compliance audits on a regular and irregular basis.
 
◈External ISO 14001 and ISO 45000 audits are performed. 
 
◈Should an environmental violation be found, the Safety and Health Department 
shall issue a notice to the complex committing the violation and include the 
complex involved in the evaluation of bonus reduction. Meanwhile, anyone who 
is found to have committed violations of environmental protection regulations 
by the competent authorities shall be dismissed from FPC in severe cases.
 
◈In addition, the Safety and Health Department holds regular internal 
regulatory forums to report the inspection results of any violation cases and 
to amend relevant management policies. All complexes and plants are also 
notified promptly to implement parallel improvements so as to prevent similar 
violations from happening again.
Stakeholder 
Engagement
Stakeholders: Residents in the Operation Area, Government Agencies, Experts, 
Scholars, and Environmental Protection Organizations, Suppliers and 
Contractors, Employees
FPC has put in place an environmental protection and pollution whistleblower 
system in accordance with the “Regulations Governing Supervision and 
Management of Environmental Protection” and encourages employees for 
reporting violations of environmental protection regulations, environmental 
pollution, etc. FPC has set up the "Contact Us" page on our official website for 
you to leave comments and file complaints.

In 2022, FPC did not receive any environmental violation ticket nor commit any major environmental 
violation (major violations are defined as single events penalized with a fine of NT$1 million or more). 
In view of various environmental protection regulations and standards as well as increasingly stringent 
penalties for violations, FPC will continue to propose improvement measures in safety, health, and 
environmental management in the future, with hopes of ensuring zero environmental violation.
3.1.3 Biodiversity
FPC attaches great importance to its impact on the surrounding environment and ecology during operation 
at the complexes and is committed to taking care of the surrounding environment and ecology. FPC has 
taken a series of progressive measures, including promoting greening and beautification projects at the 
complexes, planting trees and protecting forests outside the complexes, investigating and maintaining 
diverse biological environments, etc. Notable achievements are as follows:
1
Greening and beautiﬁcation evaluation at the complexes
Since the establishment of each complex location, where there were no natural trees around, FPC has 
developed overall plans to not only create green spaces and plant trees and flowers but also establish 
safe and green working environments through an adoption and evaluation program. Annual greening and 
beautification evaluation is performed at each complex to reward units with outstanding achievements, so 
as to encourage each complex to move towards a park-like working environment. 
2 Tree planting, forest protection, and ecological restoration outside the complexes
In addition to long-term adoption of tree planting and forest 
protection on campus of National Sun Yat-Sen University, 
FPC has also launched a Taiwanese fiddler crab conservation 
program in 2022. In view of the fact that the Zhuoshui River 
estuary on the north side of the Mailiao Industrial Park is the 
primary habitat of Taiwanese fiddler crabs, the number of 
which exceeds more than 80% of the total amount in Taiwan, 
in order to protect this rare endemic species of Taiwan, we 
have been working with Formosa Petrochemical Corporation 
and the Global Change Biology Research Center of National 
Chung Hsing University to conduct long-term 
monitoring of the mangroves, substrate composition, 
and Taiwanese fiddler crab population on the northern 
shores of the Xucuoliao Fishing Harbor, in order to 
explore the impact of the mangroves on the Taiwanese 
fiddler crab and the extent of the population dynamics, 
while promoting the conservation and environmental 
education of Taiwanese fiddler crabs at the Zhuoshui 
River estuary. 
Shih-Chang Chang, Assistant Vice President of FPC, 
signed a memorandum of understanding (MOU) 
with the Global Change Biology Research Center of 
National Chung Hsing University.
Taiwanese fiddler crabs

74
2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
3 Investigation and maintenance of diverse biological environments
In order to ensure the water quality and ecological environment of the sea area around the Mailiao 
complex, a water quality and ecological survey of the sea area is conducted every quarter. A total of 
four surveys were completed in 2022, among which the water quality survey included 34 water quality 
parameters such as water temperature, salinity, dissolved oxygen, biochemical oxygen demand, pH, 
chlorophyll A, and nutrients; the ecological survey included assessment of sediment particles diameter, 
total organic carbon and heavy metal elements, biological heavy metal elements, phytoplankton, 
zooplankton, benthos, fish caught by gillnets, mammals, etc. If you have any questions about the surveys, 
please visit the website of the Environmental Protection Administration of Executive Yuan for more 
detailed information.
Sampling of sea water quality and ecological monitoring
3.1.4 Environmental Accounting
FPG is the first enterprise in Taiwan to directly include environmental benefits into the environmental 
accounting system. FPC’s environmental costs in 2022 totaled NT$3,193 million, where the costs of green 
procurement, recycling and re-manufacturing of products produced or sold, and products and services 
derived from environmental protection initiatives amounted to NT$1,398 million, accounting for 43.8%. 
This indicates that FPC has attached great importance to environmental protection and strive to reduce 
indirect environmental impact and effects. For more information on FPC’s environmental costs in 2022 
and over the years, please refer to our Sustainable Development website.

◈Identify and manage risks and opportunities arising from climate change in
