of Diseases
Prevention of work-related cerebrovascular diseases
The “Health Care Reminder Form” is sent to employees with metabolic syndrome, with a 
follow-up examination notice sent in a confidential document, according to the abnormal 
values in the annual health checkup data and the screening results of metabolic syndrome. 
Also, relevant supervisors are notified to assist with the follow-up examination. In addition, 
our occupational health nurses track the status of the follow-up examination as well.

Strengthening Health Promotion and Awareness through Seminars
In view of the fact that metabolic syndrome accounts for most of the abnormal health conditions for 
employees in recent years, FPC not only has nurses stationed at complexes issue letter of care and notice 
of follow-up examination to employees according to their health examination results, but also progressively 
promotes classes on weight loss and smoking cessation, raises awareness of healthy diet, and enhances 
health education on chronic diseases. Moreover, doctors or instructors are invited from Chang Gung 
Memorial Hospital, the local Public Health Center, Chang Gung Biotechnology, and independent practices 
to give health talks at FPC in hopes of giving employees greater insight into how to maintain a healthy 
lifestyle that can help reduce the risk of chronic diseases such as metabolic syndrome.

Epidemic Prevention Management
In order to quickly take necessary measures in the event of an epidemic, we have established an 
epidemic response team with reference to the response to SARS and planned to announce the response 
measures. Once a case is identified, we will immediately start an investigation in accordance with the 
measures announced by the Central Epidemic Command Center (CECC) and report to our response team, 
so that control procedures for epidemic prevention leave, self-health management, and so forth can be 
formulated as soon as possible. When necessary, we also perform deep disinfection and cleaning of the 
surrounding environment.
FPC's epidemic response plan includes epidemic prevention control measures, preparation of epidemic 
prevention supplies, abnormal case tracking, personnel health care, shift management, and visitor control. 
FPC also puts great efforts into strengthening the awareness of epidemic prevention, so as to reduce the 
impact of an epidemic on business operations.
 
Occupational Injury Statistics and Descriptions
In 2022, no major occupational accidents occurred at FPC. The 
disabling injury frequency rate among employees was 0.18, 
and the disabling injury severity rate was 4, with no cases of 
occupational diseases recorded. Occupational injuries that 
occurred over the years were mainly bruises (knocks), which 
were resulted from lack of safety awareness or SOP violations 
among employees. For more details, please refer to Appendix I: 
ESG Key Performance.
With a view to ensuring that employees pay serious attention to 
the risks of occupational hazards, FPC has set relevant penalties 
for SOP violations to ensure compliance with operational safety 
rules for various operations among employees. Moreover, FPC 
promotes non-routine safety management, where supervisors 
will lead operators to conduct actual simulations of non-process 
operations with irregular cycles and intervals of more than six 
months according to SOP in order to ensure operational safety.
 
Transportation Accident
Number of transportation accidents in 2022: 1 Case
1. FPC regularly conducts the transportation contractor road transportation safety quality assessment system (SQAS) 
evaluation, and evaluates the transportation contractor's carrying quality, safety management and emergency 
response handling capabilities. Those who fail the evaluation shall not undertake our transportation business. 
In November 2022, we conducted on-site inspection of transportation vehicles and audited our transportation 
contractors. As a result, 10 abnormalities were found, mainly due to the lack of written documents and on-board 
equipment. Upon our request, the transportation contractors have completed the required improvement.
2. Each complex has professional emergency response personnel, and has set up sufficient emergency response 
equipment and vehicles. In addition, for the transportation of Class 1~3 toxic chemical substances, all members of 
the national joint defense organization shall participate in the National Joint Defense Organization in accordance with 
the provisions of the Toxic and Concerned Chemical Substances Control Act. All members of the organization are 
equipped with emergency response equipment, which can respond to emergencies in different transportation routes.
3. In order to strengthen the capability to respond to transportation emergencies and accidents, FPC requires all of 
its complexes and transportation contractors to purchase additional tank moving equipment and incorporate tank 
moving operations into the annual transportation drills, so as to increase personnel's familiarity with tank-moving 
equipment and operating procedures.

SASB Operational Safety, Emergency Preparedness & Response
Policy 
Commitments
Compliance with the Occupational Safety and Health Act, domestic laws and regulations 
relating to fire services and hazardous goods in plants, and related regulations on process 
safety management; and take responsibility for hazardous workplace management, in 
hopes of achieving the goal of “zero accidents, zero disasters”. Reduce external impact 
through this mechanism in the event of an abnormal event, so as to protect the health 
and safety of stakeholders.
Management 
Approach and 
Performance 
Monitoring
Emergency Prevention and Response
 
◈Enhance the management of emergency response and personnel training at 
complexes (departments)
 
◈Regularly organize emergency response drills every six months. The Safety 
and Health Center and the Manager's Office of various divisions at each 
complex will immediately review related deficiencies after each drill to revise 
emergency response regulations and establish SOP.
 
◈Assess emergency response measures in the early stage of accidents and 
revise emergency rescue regulations
 
◈Assess fire safety and rescue capacity, and add fire safety equipment every year
 
◈Organize joint exercises with the competent authorities on a regular basis
Public Safety at All Complexes
 
◈Pay attention to hazard prevention, implement accident investigation and 
analysis, and raise awareness of such accidents to prevent similar accidents 
in the future
 
◈Strengthen the management of process pipeline and equipment integrity
 
◈Regularly review and audit process safety assessments and the 
implementation of SOP every three years
 
◈Promote process safety management (PSM), process safety assessment, 
management of change (MOC), and pre-trip inspection, and implement SOP 
to enhance risk management and reduce the likelihood of hazard occurrence
 
◈Implement working environment and employee health management to 
reduce workplace risks and protect employees' safety and health
Overall Inspection at Mailiao Complex
Since 2022, FPG has undertaken the implementation of circular autonomous 
management for overall inspection as determined by the Industrial Development Bureau 
of the Ministry of Economic Affairs (MOEA) and scheduled to inspect 14 plants within 
3 years. As of this year, inspections at 5 plants have been completed, and competent 
authorities, experts, and scholars have been invited to supervise and provide guidance. 
There was no abnormality detected and no fine was imposed based on the inspection 
results. However, 181 improvement suggestions were provided (96 for process safety, 68 
for environmental protection, and 17 for energy), of which 143 improvement items have 
been completed, and the remaining 38 improvement items are in progress.

Emergency Response at Complexes
A. Emergency Response Mechanism
FPC divides its emergency response mechanism into three stages. In the event of an accident, it will be 
reported immediately according to the reporting procedure, followed by the activation of the emergency 
response mechanism. An emergency commander is assigned at each stage. The regional defense 
organization within the complex may be launched as needed to support disaster relief at plants in the 
vicinity. Any accidents are reported to the competent authority within the statutory time limit. 
Emergency Response Mechanisms
Incident Reporting Procedures

Stage 2
Stage 3

alarms, pollution or other accidents 
at a complex can be handled by the 
emergency response organization.
Large-scale leaks, fire alarms, 
explosions, or accidents that tend 
to expand after immediate 
response at a complex are handled 
by the emergency response 
organization at the complex.
Accidents that have spread 
outside the complex and posed a 
serious threat to the residents 
should be handled by the 
emergency response organization 
and the competent authorities.

"Emergency Response at All Complexes"  
 
◈Each complex regularly convenes Occupational Safety and Health Committee 
meetings each quarter. Proposal on matters involving emergency response that 
require handling and coordination can be raised in these meetings, and the head 
of the President's Office at Complex (i.e. the chairperson of the committee) will 
make decisions on the relevant solutions in these meetings.
 
◈Each unit can personally notify the Safety and Health Department of other 
aperiodic cases for further action.
"Public Safety at All Complexes"

message on the Company's official website. FPC will assign a dedicated unit or 
personnel to reply according to the type of question raised.

B. Results of the Drills at Each Complex
To enhance fire safety and disaster relief capabilities, each complex arranges fire and rescue emergency 
response drills in different scenarios every six months. Additionally, each complex also carries out overall 
and no-warning test drills on EPA's controlled chemicals, including complexes and transportation. On 
September 23, 2022, we worked with the Kaohsiung City Government to conduct the "2022 Kaohsiung City 
Toxic Chemical Disaster Joint Prevention Team Emergency Response Drill".

4.4 Supply Chain Management
4.4.1 Supplier and Contractor Management
2022 CDP Supply Chain Project Score: “A”
According to the CDP Score 
Report - Supply Chain 2022, FPC 
was rated A (Leadership). This 
demonstrates our efforts to lead the 
upstream and downstream supply 
chains and implement sustainable 
supply chain management.
(1) Supplier and Contractor Management
Upholding the spirit of sustainable development and the principle of fair trade, FPC urges that all suppliers 
and contractors should meet the requirements for environmental protection, industrial safety, and human 
rights. Since October 2019, FPC has added the Supplier/Contractor Social Responsibility Commitment and 
the Supplier/Contractor Social Responsibility Questionnaire, requesting suppliers and contractors to sign 
and respond to the aforesaid commitment and questionnaire upon signing in to the Formosa Technology 
E-Market Place or ordering. By 2022, we had a total of 2,545 domestic partnered manufacturers, of 
which 2,529 have signed the Social Responsibility Commitment, with a response rate of 99.4%; 2,443 have 
completed the Social Responsibility Questionnaire, with a response rate of 95.9%.

and should be signed and returned. The signing statistics have been collected since 2021. Among the 2,545 
domestic partnered manufacturers in 2022, 2,522 have signed, with a response rate of 99.1%.

(2) Supplier/Contractor Evaluation and Category Management
FPC continues to conduct rating assessments for material suppliers and conducts manufacturer 
evaluations as needed to ensure that suppliers are able to meet our requirements to fulfill corporate 
sustainability responsibilities. In 2022, a total of 9,261 suppliers received rating assessments. Among them, 
9,196 suppliers (rated A to E) are determined to be sustainable, accounting for 99.29%. For the remaining 
65 (rated F) suppliers, which accounts for 0.71%, as they failed to meet the assessment standards, we 
have ended our partnership.

Supplier Assessment
Supplier Rating
FPC evaluates major suppliers of various materials. The procurement department and material 
department work together to collect relevant information, including manufacturing scale, production 
capacity, sales amount, and quality certification, as well as require manufacturers to abide by relevant 
regulations such as environmental protection, industrial safety, and human rights. Meanwhile, we work 
with the material department to establish assessment items and rating standards and conduct written and 
on-site factory assessments for suppliers:
We collect the quotation data and delivery records of manufacturers in the past two years every month to calculate 
rating. Every quarter, each material department determines the levels of manufacturers based on not only 
the quality, durability, and after-sales service of important 
materials but also the implementation of the manufacturers 
in terms of environmental protection, industrial safety, and 
human rights protection, so as to provide reference for pricing 
comparison and procurement decision making:

2022 Formosa Plastics Corporation　Sustainability Report
FPC has also established the incentive system for suppliers/contractors. 
Besides from ensuring that all manufacturers can abide to company 
regulations, by turning penalties into rewards, FPC evaluates the safety 
and health management performance of contractors on a regular basis 
and grants rewards based on the results of the evaluation to encourage 
contractors' self-initiated management on industrial safety and to raise 
their safety awareness.
For more information on supplier/contractor evaluation and grading 
management, please refer to FPC’s Sustainable Development website. 
4.4.2 Supplier/Contractor Injury Indicators
To improve the workplace safety of the supply chain, FPC also requires that all suppliers and contractors 
should report relevant data on occupational injuries. In 2022, the total number of people included in the 
statistics was 4,030, and no major occupational disaster occurred. The occupational injuries that occurred 
over the years were mainly pinches, scalds, and splashes of hazardous materials. We have reminded 
all suppliers and contractors to pay attention to work safety rules and comply with workplace safety 
regulations to reduce the risk of occupational hazards. Injury indicators for suppliers and contractors in 
2022 are described as follows:

4.4.3 Procurement Policy
FPC adopts an “open tender” approach and implements 
it via the Formosa Technology E-Market Place, which 
enables both suppliers and contractors to carry out 
various operations, such as price quotation, inquiry, 
and negotiation. Regular meetings with contractors and 
suppliers are also organized to encourage and enhance 
two-way communication.

 To reduce carbon emissions from delivery vehicles, FPC has collaborated with Kerry TJ Logistics to promote 
the "Supplier Collaboration E-System."
 To further reduce invoice costs and increase the efficiency of invoice management, electronic invoices have 
been promoted to comprehensively replace traditional paper invoices.
 The procurement and outsourcing policies mainly revolve around local procurement and outsourcing. FPC 
only sources goods from overseas and allows bidding from abroad when local suppliers are unable to meet 
the needs.
 FPC actively promotes green procurement and has cooperated with the Taipei City Government to sign its

5.1 Local Community Development

5.1.1 Community Relations
In order to maintain a good interaction with the local community and create a family tie between the 
complexes and nearby villages, FPC is willing to assist neighboring groups and organizations around our 
complexes to organize local events or social welfare activities. Affected by the COVID-19 pandemic in 2022, 
the Company is adjusting its activities in line with government policies and continues to fulfill its original 
mission of giving back to its neighbors under the premise of taking proper epidemic prevention measures 
and avoiding clusters. For more local events, please refer to the "Latest News in FPC" on our Sustainable 
Development website.

Stakeholder Feedback
Shu-Ya Xie, Deputy Magistrate of Yunlin County Government:
We would like to thank FPG for giving back to the local 
community. In addition to assisting farmers in selling Douliu 
Wendan (pomelo) at today's event, what we hope most is to 
promote and sell quality Douliu Wendan (pomelo) to everywhere 
in Taiwan. Through collaboration with businesses to assist in 
the marketing of local agricultural products, we not only provide 
direct support for farmers in Yunlin but also join efforts to 
promote corporate brands, so as to establish a better channel 
for cooperation between businesses and farmers in Yunlin.
Clean Home - Beach Cleanups
Shu-Ya Xie, Deputy Magistrate of Yunlin County Government:
In order to prevent pollution sources such as waste fishing 
nets and waste from entering the ocean, the Yunlin County 
Government has strengthened control over ghost nets and marine 
debris in recent years. In addition to a planned temporary storage 
area for marine debris, a real-name system for gillnet fishing 
gear, and the promotion of reuse of waste clams, the Yunlin 
County Government also proactively encourages businesses 
and organizations to adopt coastlines and participate in beach 
cleanups to remove litter, so as to reduce marine pollution by 
implementing concrete environmental protection actions.

5.1.2 Complex Operations and Community Relations
 
Operational Impact Management
Operational 
Impact
Impact Identiﬁcation
Community Engagement 
Water 
Usage
  According to the “Jiji Weir Industrial and Public Water 
Supply Monthly Report” issued by the Industrial 
Development Bureau, Ministry of Economic Affairs, the 
annual water supply of Jiji Weir from 2019 to 2022 ranged 
from 175,073 to 510,006 megatons. The average industrial 
water use accounts for 3.1% of the average total water 
supply; the average agricultural water transfer accounts 
for only 2.3% of the average total agricultural water use, 
indicating that the water consumption at the Mailiao 
Park does not supplant other industries nor result in 
competition for water with farmers.
  For the statistics of water supplied by Jiji Weir from 2019 
to 2022, please refer to Appendix I: ESG Key Performance. 
  The Safety, Health and Environment Center 
conducts public presentations every year to 
showcase the excellent water-saving improvement 
cases within FPG. The continuous exchange 
of water-saving technologies and professional 
knowledge is not only beneficial for companies in 
the Group to learn from each other, but also to the 
external departments and residents participating in 
the meeting.
  Residents outside the Company can directly 
report various issues related to water resources 
management to the plant management department.
Air 
Pollution
  According to the 2019 air pollutant emissions data 
inventory from the Taiwan Emissions Data System 
(TEDS) 11.1 version released by the Environmental 
Protection Administration (EPA), for example, the 
total amount of air pollutant emissions for all of 
FPC’s Kaohsiung complexes in 2019 accounted for 
0.21% to 4.70% of the total amount of air pollutants 
in Kaohsiung City, showing that the air pollutant 
emissions of FPC’s complexes are not a significant 
source of the city’s overall emissions.
  An air quality monitoring board has been 
installed at the entrance of the Renwu 
Complex to display real-time air quality data 
through continuous and automatic monitoring 
for the public to view. Additionally, a detailed 
explanation of the reasons for using the gas 
flare is available on FPG’s Air Pollution Incident 
Control Website.
  Our air quality monitoring results inside and 
outside the complex are regularly submitted to 
the village head office for inspection. We also 
visit other village heads of nearby areas from 
time to time to report the progress and results 
of recent improvements in environmental 
protection (including air pollution). On January 
6, 2023, Chairman Lin reported to the village 
heads in the southern complex areas and local 
residents on the environmental protection 
performance of the Renwu Complex and 
Linyuan Complex in recent years, such as the 
discharge of waste water into the sea and the 
elimination of white smoke from chimneys.
  Residents outside FPC can directly report 
various issues related to air pollution 
management to the Safety and Health 
Department/Office at the complexes.
  In 2022, no reports or complaints about air 
pollution from residents or organizations have 
been received at FPC.
Public 
Safety 
at All 
Complexes
  In view of the fact that major fire accidents across 
the world are all related to storage management 
of public hazardous materials, in order to ensure 
the safety management of the storage areas of public 
hazardous materials at each unit, we have performed 
inspections for 202 controlled areas.
  In accordance with the Fire Services Act Amendment 
Bill, for outdoor storage tanks of liquid hazardous 
materials  1,000 kiloliter, an internal inspection is 
required every five years.
  In order to prevent continuous leakage of flammable, 
explosive toxic substance pipelines or equipment, 
non-preventive or preventive materials or devices are 
used to prevent leakage.
  Depending on the circumstances, the 
Mailiao Administration Department may 
send a “safety text message” to inform local 
residents on behalf of the Mailiao Complex.
  Depending on the circumstances, complexes 
other than Mailiao may make notification by 
telephone first and then by fax.
  Residents outside FPC can directly report 
various issues related to public safety to 
the Administration Department at each 
complex.

Public Welfare Engagement
To have an in-depth understanding of social needs, FPC actively 
cooperates with the public and private sectors to invest human 
resources and funds in promoting local developments and 
philanthropic activities, including community activities, road 
maintenance, education, care for the elderly, cultural promotion, 
charities, temple activities and more. In order to encourage the 
development of local cultures, in 2022, we invested a total of more 
than NT$1.45 million in arts and cultural events, such as musicals 
performed by the YunLin Philharmonic Chamber Choir, flower drum 
cultural events, dance contests, and concerts. 
Moreover, Formosa Wang Brothers Park was registered as a heritage asset by the Kaohsiung City 
Government on December 5, 2018, and the Kaohsiung City Wang Yung-ching & Wang Yung-tsai Brotherhood 
Park Foundation was co-founded by FPC, NPC, 
FCFC, and FPCC. We donated NT$84.976 million 
to the foundation in 2022 for the planning, design, 
and construction of the restoration and reuse of 
cultural assets in the park, so as to contribute to 
the preservation of cultural heritage. In celebration 
of the International Day for Monuments and Sites 
on April 18 each year, we have joined forces 
with the Bureau of Cultural Affairs of Kaohsiung 
City Government to organize a cultural heritage 
carnival from April 15 to 16, 2023, and an official 
announcement was made to invite the public to 
participate. The carnival included a number of 
activities, such as themed markets, professional 
lectures, guided tours, music performances, 
forums on archaeological sites, performances of 
war drum skills, etc. For more details, please go to 
the Formosa Wang Brothers Park official website
For more information on FPG's social investments 
and expenditures, please visit FPG's official website.
5.2 Community Engagement
5.2.1 Industry-Academia Collaboration
FPC actively establishes industry-academia collaboration with various universities and colleges and 
arranges students to work and undergo practical training at our complexes and departments, with a view 
to supporting local education, enhancing students' practical work experience, and reducing emigration. 
The situation of industry-academia collaboration in 2022 are described below.

5.2.2 Formosa LOHAS Circle
Formosa LOHAS Circle activities are mainly

and Kaohsiung. Focusing on environmental 
sustainability and social engagement, FPC 
has promoted the Formosa LOHAS Circle in 
cooperation with local communities, vendors, 
small farmers, and local governments around 
the complexes. For more information, please 
refer to the website of Formosa LOHAS Circle.
5.2.3  Other Engagement Actions
 
Mailiao Social Education Park
FPG started investment in Mailiao Township, Yunlin County in 1994. 
Adhering to the principles of “Diligence, Perseverance, Frugality, 
and Trustworthiness” we devote all our resources to assist local 
authorities in completing various infrastructure projects, which not 
only promotes local development but also significantly improves 
the living standards and social welfare of local residents. The 
population growth rate of Mailiao Township has been rising year 
after year, and it has become the third largest township in Yunlin 
County after Douliu City and Huwei Township.

In addition, we have long been committed to 
promoting neighborliness and social welfare and 
have been doing our best to give back to local 
communities. We have invested NT$479 million 
to build the Mailiao Social Education Park, with a 
construction area of 3,229 Taiwanese pings. The 
park has become a diverse venue for books and 
arts events, social education studies, and leisure 
activities. The architecture of the park combines 
traditional cultural elements of Mailiao and modern 
aesthetics, coupled with green building design, and 
we hope that the Mailiao Social Education Park will 
develop into a new landmark of Mailiao.
 
PRAY FOR TURKEY
In the early hours of February 6, 2023, a magnitude 7.8 earthquake occurred in 
Kahramanmaras Province in southeastern Turkey, affecting many surrounding 
cities including Gaziantep. Followed by continuous aftershocks, the country 
suffered heavy casualties, and the scale of this disaster shocked and saddened 
the whole world. In view of the shortage of supplies after the disaster in Turkey, 
to fulfill corporate citizenship, we immediately raised 500 units of warm jackets, 
blankets, and thermos bottles and delivered them to Turkey as soon as possible 
for the victims to stay warm in winter. We sincerely hope that Turkey is able to 
rebuild and that the injured recover and return to normal life as soon as possible.

Note 1: Permanent employee: employee with a contract for an indeterminate period (i.e., indefinite contract) for full-time or part-time work
Note 2: Temporary employee: employee with a contract for a limited period (i.e., fixed term contract). The contract ends when the specific time period expires, 
or when the specific task or event that has an attached time estimate is completed (e.g., the end of a project or return of replaced employees).
Note 3: Full-time employee: employee whose working hours per week, month, or year are defined according to national law or practice regarding working time
Note 4: Part-time employee: employee whose working hours per week, month, or year are less than the number of working hours for full-time employees
Note 5: Non-guaranteed hours employee: employee who is not guaranteed a minimum or fixed number of working hours per day, week, or month, but who 
may need to make themselves available for work as required

Note 1: The fatality caused by occupational injuries is the number of deaths per million hours worked, and the formula is: Number of deaths caused by 
occupational injuries x 1,000,000 ÷ Hours worked
Note 2: Disabling Injury Severity Rate (SR) is the number of days of disability (including death) per million hours worked, and the formula is: total lost 
days x 1,000,000 ÷ hours worked
Note 3: Disability frequency (FR), which is the number of times of disability (including death) per million working hours, the formula is: total number of 
lost persons x 1,000,000 ÷ number of working hours
Note 4: Recordable occupational injury rate: It is the number of recordable occupational injuries that occurred within one million working hours, 
including the number of deaths and the number of disability injuries. The formula is: Number of recordable occupational injuries x 1,000,000 ÷ 
number of working hours
Note 5: FPC started to compile data on the "severity of disability injuries" of subcontractors in 2021.
Note 6: In 2022, there was no cases of major occupational accidents or occupational diseases in 2022.

RT-CH-140a.3
Description of water 
management risks and 
discussion of strategies and 
practices to mitigate those 
risks
 Improvement in water and energy conservation: The 
President's Office and the President's Office at Complex 
regularly conduct review with the Safety, Health and 
Environment Center under the Group Administration 
Office to keep track of each company's water conservation 
performance and formulate implementation approaches.
 Performance evaluation of water resources management: 
The President's Office at various complexes conducts 
the performance evaluation of energy conservation and 
carbon reduction every month to reward the best complex/
department. In 2022, the best-performing complex/
department was Mailiao HDPE Plant, which received a 
bonus of NT$50,000.
 Circular economy performance presentation: The 
Safety, Health and Environment Center organizes public 
presentations each year to showcase outstanding water 
conservation improvement projects at each company 
under FPG and exchange water conservation technologies 
and related professional knowledge.

Disclosure 
Topic
Community Relations
Indicator Code
Disclosure Indicator
Comparison Disclosure
Reference 
Chapter
RT-CH-210a.1
Discussion of engagement 
processes to manage risks and 
opportunities associated with 
community interests
  The use and management of various water resources 
shall strictly comply with legal requirements.
  The Safety, Health and Environment Center conducts 
public presentations every year to showcase the 
excellent water-saving improvement cases in 
the enterprise (all companies must present their 
information). The continuous exchange of water-
saving technologies and professional knowledge is 
not only beneficial to the company, but also to the 
external departments and residents participating in 
the meeting.
  Residents outside the Company can directly 
report various issues related to water resources 
management to the plant management department.
  According to the data given by the Ministry of 
Economic Affairs, annual water supply of Jiji Weir in 
the past four years (2019-2022) ranged from 175,073 
to 510,006 megatons. The average of industrial 
water consumption accounted for 3.1% of the total 
water supply, while water consumption transferred 
from agricultural water usage only accounted 
for 2.3%, demonstrating that the water for the 
Mailiao Park does not compete with the farmers 
for water. In order to effectively utilize Taiwan's 
precious water resources, FPC not only strives for 
process improvement, enhancement of equipment 
effectiveness, optimization of operating conditions, 
and recycling and reuse of wastewater to increase 
water use efficiency, but also promotes recycling and 
reuse of rainwater at the same time.

Revenue from products designed 
for use-phase resource efficiency 
(Unit: NT$)
FPC continues to invest in the development of new 
and forward-looking, differentiated, and products and 
technologies with high value, and actively develops 
differentiated and green material products. A total 
of 32 new products were developed in 2022, with a 
potential annual benefit of NT$ 410,178 thousand. 12 
of the new products were commercialized in 2022, 
with a total revenue of NT$621,800 thousand.

RT-CH-320a.2
Efforts to reduce 
exposure of employees to 
occupational health risks
 Set relevant penalties for SOP violations to ensure 
compliance with operational safety rules for various 
operations among employees
 Promote non-routine safety management, where 
supervisors will lead operators to conduct actual 
simulations of non-process operations with irregular 
cycles and intervals of more than six months according 
to SOP in order to ensure operational safety
Disclosure 
Topic
Management of the Legal & Regulatory Environment
Indicator Code
Disclosure Indicator
Comparison Disclosure
Reference 
Chapter
RT-CH-530a.1
Discussion of corporate positions 
related to government regulations 
and/or policy proposals that 
address environmental and social 
factors affecting the industry
1. FPC has established the “Regulations Governing 
Supervision and Management of Environmental 
Protection”, which stipulates that employees at 
all levels shall fulfill environmental protection-
related duties, and that the Safety and Health 
Department, the Safety and Health Team at each 
division, and environmental protection personnel 
at each complex and department shall conduct 
environmental protection compliance audits on a 
regular and irregular basis. In 2022, FPC did not 
receive any environmental violation ticket, and 
there was no major environmental violation.
2. When government agencies invite experts, 
scholars, and environmental protection 
organizations to conduct general inspections of 
industrial safety and environmental protection, FPC 
discusses and responds to the review opinions of 
experts, scholars, and environmental protection 
organizations.
3. FPC is an active member of the Chinese National 
Federation of Industries (CNFI). FPC is also a 
member of the Sustainability Committee and 
the Environmental Protection Committee of the 
Petrochemical Industry Association of Taiwan 
(PIAT), representing the Petrochemical Industry 
Association of Taiwan (PIAT) to participate in 
various conferences on safety, health, environment, 
and sustainability and to seek recognition of 
experts, scholars, and environmental organizations 
for the petrochemical industry.

RT-CH-410b.2
Describe the management 
strategy for chemicals
Ensure the safety of workplaces of hazardous 
substances (including chemical substances and 
hazardous chemical substances listed by the 
Environmental Protection Agency). In addition to 
requiring the responsible personnel to obtain technical 
licenses and to install detection and alarm equipment 
systems in the plant; for the unused chemical 
substances listed by the Environmental Protection 
Agency, after declaring their disposal according to the 
law, they will be treated as hazardous industrial wastes 
and managed properly.
Describe strategies for 
developing alternatives with 
reduced impact on humans and/
or the environment
 Adjust the freezing temperature of the process and 
change to the low-hazard refrigerant: Originally, the 
ODS refrigerant such as CFC-11/12/22 was in use, 
after the improvement of the process, the freezing 
temperature of the process is being adjusted and the 
refrigerant material to non-toxic propylene, R134a 
and other low-hazard refrigerants are adopted.
 Turn off the processes with high greenhouse gas: 
such as closing the production NF3 process.
 Adjust the catalyst solvent in the process: if the 
original catalyst solvent is heptane (a dangerous 
article), replace it with low-hazard white oil.
 Develop toxic solvent substitutes: During the 
production of carbon fibers, DMSO solvents is used 
to replace DMF solvents.

Strategies, methods and 
goals of greenhouse gas 
management
Qualitative 
narrative
FPC has set an absolute target 
for GHG emission reduction with 
the base year of 2020 (8.635 
million tons CO2e). In particular, 
GHG emissions will be reduced 
by 20% in 2025 compared to the 
base year, and by 40% in 2030 
compared to the base year, with 
the goal of achieving carbon 
neutrality by 2050.

to produce FPC’s recycled PP 
woven bags.
